One last sanity check on the T2 center computation:
T2 at Q=(u,v,w)*step:
Vertices: (u,v,w), (u+1,v+1,w), (u+1,v,w-1), (u,v+1,w-1) all × step
Center = ((u+u+1+u+1+u)/4, (v+v+1+v+v+1)/4, (w+w+w-1+w-1)/4) × step
       = ((4u+2)/4, (4v+2)/4, (4w-2)/4) × step
       = (u+0.5, v+0.5, w-0.5) × step
       = (qu+r, qv+r, qw-r) ✓ (since r=step/2)

This is what I output for T2: {qu+r, qv+r, qw-r}. ✓

Now let me write the final code:

```cpp
#include <cstdio>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <array>
#include <algorithm>

using namespace std;
typedef array<double,3> V3;
typedef array<array<double,3>,3> M3;

// Vector operations
V3 add(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]+b[0],a[1]+b[1],a[2]+b[2]};}
V3 sub(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]-b[0],a[1]-b[1],a[2]-b[2]};}
V3 scl(double s,V3 a){return{s*a[0],s*a[1],s*a[2]};}
double dot(V3 a,V3 b){return a[0]*b[0]+a[1]*b[1]+a[2]*b[2];}
V3 crs(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[1]*b[2]-a[2]*b[1],a[2]*b[0]-a[0]*b[2],a[0]*b[1]-a[1]*b[0]};}
double nrm(V3 a){return sqrt(dot(a,a));}
V3 nml(V3 a){double n=nrm(a);return n<1e-14?V3{0,0,0}:scl(1/n,a);}

// Matrix operations
M3 mmul(M3 a,M3 b){M3 r{};for(int i=0;i<3;i++)for(int j=0;j<3;j++)for(int k=0;k<3;k++)r[i][j]+=a[i][k]*b[k][j];return r;}
double det3(M3 m){return m[0][0]*(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])-m[0][1]*(m[1][0]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][0])+m[0][2]*(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0]);}
M3 inv3(M3 m){
    double d=det3(m);
    return{{{(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])/d,(m[0][2]*m[2][1]-m[0][1]*m[2][2])/d,(m[0][1]*m[1][2]-m[0][2]*m[1][1])/d},
            {(m[1][2]*m[2][0]-m[1][0]*m[2][2])/d,(m[0][0]*m[2][2]-m[0][2]*m[2][0])/d,(m[0][2]*m[1][0]-m[0][0]*m[1][2])/d},
            {(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0])/d,(m[0][1]*m[2][0]-m[0][0]*m[2][1])/d,(m[0][0]*m[1][1]-m[0][1]*m[1][0])/d}}};
}

// ZYX Euler angles from rotation matrix
array<double,3> toEuler(M3 R){
    double ry=asin(max(-1.0,min(1.0,-R[2][0])));
    double cy=cos(ry),rx,rz;
    if(fabs(cy)>1e-7){rx=atan2(R[2][1]/cy,R[2][2]/cy);rz=atan2(R[1][0]/cy,R[0][0]/cy);}
    else{rx=0;rz=atan2(-R[0][1],R[1][1]);}
    return{rx,ry,rz};
}

// Build rotation from canonical tet to target tet
// Canonical (e=edge_len, centered at origin):
// v0=(0,0,e*sqrt(6)/4), v1=(0,e/sqrt(3),-e*sqrt(6)/12),
// v2=(-e/2,-e/(2*sqrt(3)),-e*sqrt(6)/12), v3=(e/2,-e/(2*sqrt(3)),-e*sqrt(6)/12)
M3 buildRotMat(double e,V3 t0,V3 t1,V3 t2,V3 t3){
    const double s3=sqrt(3.0),s6=sqrt(6.0);
    V3 v0={0,0,e*s6/4};
    V3 v1={0,e/s3,-e*s6/12};
    V3 v2={-e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    V3 v3={e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    V3 b1=sub(v1,v0),b2=sub(v2,v0),b3=sub(v3,v0);
    M3 B={{{b1[0],b2[0],b3[0]},{b1[1],b2[1],b3[1]},{b1[2],b2[2],b3[2]}}};
    V3 a1=sub(t1,t0),a2=sub(t2,t0),a3=sub(t3,t0);
    M3 A={{{a1[0],a2[0],a3[0]},{a1[1],a2[1],a3[1]},{a1[2],a2[2],a3[2]}}};
    return mmul(A,inv3(B));
}

// Half-space: dot(n,p) >= d means inside
struct HS{V3 n;double d;};

vector<HS> convexHull(const vector<V3>& pts){
    int n=pts.size();
    V3 cen={0,0,0};
    for(auto& p:pts){cen[0]+=p[0];cen[1]+=p[1];cen[2]+=p[2];}
    cen=scl(1.0/n,cen);
    
    vector<HS> hs;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    for(int j=i+1;j<n;j++)
    for(int k=j+1;k<n;k++){
        V3 nn=nml(crs(sub(pts[j],pts[i]),sub(pts[k],pts[i])));
        if(nrm(nn)<0.5) continue; // degenerate
        double di=dot(nn,pts[i]);
        bool ok=true;
        int side=0;
        for(int l=0;l<n&&ok;l++){
            if(l==i||l==j||l==k) continue;
            double v=dot(nn,pts[l])-di;
            if(fabs(v)<1e-9) continue;
            int s=(v>0)?1:-1;
            if(!side) side=s;
            else if(s!=side) ok=false;
        }
        if(!ok) continue;
        // Make normal point toward centroid (inward)
        if(dot(nn,cen)<di){nn=scl(-1,nn);di=-di;}
        // Deduplicate
        bool dup=false;
        for(auto& h:hs)
            if(fabs(dot(h.n,nn)-1)<1e-6&&fabs(h.d-di)<1e-6){dup=true;break;}
        if(!dup) hs.push_back({nn,di});
    }
    return hs;
}

inline bool inside(const vector<HS>& hs,const V3& p,double eps=1e-7){
    for(auto& h:hs)
        if(dot(h.n,p)<h.d-eps) return false;
    return true;
}

// Fast output
static char outbuf[1<<25]; // 32MB buffer
static int outpos=0;
void oflush(){fwrite(outbuf,1,outpos,stdout);outpos=0;}
void ochar(char c){if(outpos>=(1<<25)-256)oflush();outbuf[outpos++]=c;}
void odbl(double x){
    char t[40];
    int n=sprintf(t,"%.10f",x);
    if(outpos+n>=(1<<25)-256)oflush();
    memcpy(outbuf+outpos,t,n);
    outpos+=n;
}
void oint(long long x){
    char t[32];
    int n=sprintf(t,"%lld",x);
    if(outpos+n>=(1<<25)-256)oflush();
    memcpy(outbuf+outpos,t,n);
    outpos+=n;
}

int main(){
    int V; double e;
    scanf("%d %lf",&V,&e);
    
    vector<V3> pts(V);
    for(int i=0;i<V;i++) scanf("%lf %lf %lf",&pts[i][0],&pts[i][1],&pts[i][2]);
    
    if(V<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    auto hs=convexHull(pts);
    if(hs.empty()){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    // Bounding box
    V3 lo={1e18,1e18,1e18},hi={-1e18,-1e18,-1e18};
    for(auto& p:pts)
        for(int d=0;d<3;d++){lo[d]=min(lo[d],p[d]);hi[d]=max(hi[d],p[d]);}
    
    // FCC lattice
    const double S2=sqrt(2.0);
    double step=e/S2;  // lattice spacing
    double r=step*0.5; // = e/(2*sqrt(2))
    
    // T1 centered vertices: {(-r,-r,-r),(r,r,-r),(r,-r,r),(-r,r,r)}
    V3 C1[4]={{-r,-r,-r},{r,r,-r},{r,-r,r},{-r,r,r}};
    // T2 centered vertices: {(-r,-r,r),(r,r,r),(r,-r,-r),(-r,r,-r)}
    V3 C2[4]={{-r,-r,r},{r,r,r},{r,-r,-r},{-r,r,-r}};
    
    // Build rotation matrices (swap C2[2],C2[3] for proper rotation det=+1)
    M3 R1=buildRotMat(e,C1[0],C1[1],C1[2],C1[3]);
    M3 R2=buildRotMat(e,C2[0],C2[1],C2[3],C2[2]);
    
    auto eu1=toEuler(R1);
    auto eu2=toEuler(R2);
    
    // Lattice bounds
    int umin=(int)floor(lo[0]/step)-2,umax=(int)ceil(hi[0]/step)+2;
    int vmin=(int)floor(lo[1]/step)-2,vmax=(int)ceil(hi[1]/step)+2;
    int wmin=(int)floor(lo[2]/step)-2,wmax=(int)ceil(hi[2]/step)+2;
    
    // Two-pass: count then output
    long long cnt=0;
    
    for(int u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(int v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(int w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1) continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                // T1
                {
                    V3 p0={qu,qv,qw};
                    V3 p1={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
                    V3 p2={qu+step,qv,qw+step};
                    V3 p3={qu,qv+step,qw+step};
                    if(inside(hs,p0)&&inside(hs,p1)&&inside(hs,p2)&&inside(hs,p3)) cnt++;
                }
                // T2
                {
                    V3 p0={qu,qv,qw};
                    V3 p1={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
                    V3 p2={qu+step,qv,qw-step};
                    V3 p3={qu,qv+step,qw-step};
                    if(inside(hs,p0)&&inside(hs,p1)&&inside(hs,p2)&&inside(hs,p3)) cnt++;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    oint(cnt); ochar('\n');
    
    // Output pass
    for(int u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(int v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(int w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1) continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                // T1
                {
                    V3 p0={qu,qv,qw};
                    V3 p1={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
                    V3 p2={qu+step,qv,qw+step};
                    V3 p3={qu,qv+step,qw+step};
                    if(inside(hs,p0)&&inside(hs,p1)&&inside(hs,p2)&&inside(hs,p3)){
                        odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw+r);ochar(' ');
                        odbl(eu1[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[2]);ochar('\n');
                    }
                }
                // T2
                {
                    V3 p0={qu,qv,qw};
                    V3 p1={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
                    V3 p2={qu+step,qv,qw-step};
                    V3 p3={qu,qv+step,qw-step};
                    if(inside(hs,p0)&&inside(hs,p1)&&inside(hs,p2)&&inside(hs,p3)){
                        odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw-r);ochar(' ');
                        odbl(eu2[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[2]);ochar('\n');
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    oflush();
    return 0;
}
```

This is clean and correct. But it does the work twice. For the performance constraint, let me think:
- For a container of linear size L (in units of e): step = e/√2, so L/step = L√2/e steps per dimension
- Total lattice points: (L√2/e)^3 / 2 (factor /2 for parity)
- For L/e = 100: ~10^6 points × 2 passes = ~2×10^6 iterations
- For L/e = 500: ~10^8 points × 2 passes = ~2×10^8 iterations (few seconds)
- For L/e = 1000: ~8×10^8 points × 2 passes = ~1.6×10^9 iterations (maybe 10-15 seconds single-threaded)

For "ludicrous scale" (L/e = 2000), this would be too slow. I need parallelism.

Let me add OpenMP with careful thread safety. For the count pass, use a reduction. For the output pass, use parallel threads writing to separate buffers, then combine.

Actually, for the output pass: if I allow non-deterministic ordering (just need count to be correct), I can parallelize:

```cpp
#pragma omp parallel
{
    vector<...> local_results;
    #pragma omp for schedule(dynamic,4) collapse(2)
    for(u=...) for(v=...) for(w=...) {
        // check and add to local_results
    }
    #pragma omp critical
    {
        // flush local_results to output
    }
}
```

This would work but requires careful buffer management. Let me implement it.

Actually, let me step back. The problem says output is "Lines 2..K+1: cx cy cz rx ry rz". The ordering of these lines doesn't matter (we just need K correct placements). So parallel output is fine.

For OpenMP parallel output:
- Each thread has a local buffer
- At the end, all buffers are written to stdout in some order
- The total count matches K

Here's the parallel approach:

```cpp
// Count pass (parallel)
long long cnt = 0;
#pragma omp parallel for reduction(+:cnt) schedule(dynamic,4) collapse(2)
for(int u=umin;u<=umax;u++)
for(int v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
    for(int w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
        if((u+v+w)&1) continue;
        // check T1, T2, increment cnt
    }
}

// Output count
oint(cnt); ochar('\n');

// Output pass (parallel per-thread buffers)
int nthreads;
#pragma omp parallel
{
    #pragma omp single
    nthreads = omp_get_num_threads();
}

vector<vector<char>> thread_bufs(nthreads);
for(auto& tb : thread_bufs) tb.reserve(1<<20);

#pragma omp parallel schedule(dynamic,4) collapse(2)
for(int u=umin;u<=umax;u++)
for(int v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
    int tid = omp_get_thread_num();
    for(int w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
        if((u+v+w)&1) continue;
        // write T1, T2 results to thread_bufs[tid]
    }
}

// Flush all thread buffers
for(auto& tb : thread_bufs) fwrite(tb.data(),1,tb.size(),stdout);
```

This is more complex but handles large cases. Let me implement it.

Actually, with 64 threads, the per-thread buffers could be large. If there are 10M tets total, each thread has ~156K tets × ~70 chars = ~11MB per thread = 700MB total. Fine for 127GB RAM.

Let me write the final code with OpenMP support:

```cpp
#ifdef _OPENMP
#include <omp.h>
#endif
```

And the parallel loops.

OK I've been going back and forth. Let me just WRITE THE FINAL CODE and be done with it. Here it is:

```cpp
#include <cstdio>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <array>
#include <algorithm>
#include <cstring>
#include <string>

using namespace std;
typedef array<double,3> V3;
typedef array<array<double,3>,3> M3;

V3 vadd(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]+b[0],a[1]+b[1],a[2]+b[2]};}
V3 vsub(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]-b[0],a[1]-b[1],a[2]-b[2]};}
V3 vscl(double s,V3 a){return{s*a[0],s*a[1],s*a[2]};}
double vdot(V3 a,V3 b){return a[0]*b[0]+a[1]*b[1]+a[2]*b[2];}
V3 vcrs(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[1]*b[2]-a[2]*b[1],a[2]*b[0]-a[0]*b[2],a[0]*b[1]-a[1]*b[0]};}
double vnrm(V3 a){return sqrt(vdot(a,a));}
V3 vnml(V3 a){double n=vnrm(a);return n<1e-14?V3{0,0,0}:vscl(1/n,a);}

M3 mmul(M3 a,M3 b){M3 r{};for(int i=0;i<3;i++)for(int j=0;j<3;j++)for(int k=0;k<3;k++)r[i][j]+=a[i][k]*b[k][j];return r;}
double mdet(M3 m){return m[0][0]*(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])-m[0][1]*(m[1][0]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][0])+m[0][2]*(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0]);}
M3 minv(M3 m){
    double d=mdet(m);
    return{{{(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])/d,(m[0][2]*m[2][1]-m[0][1]*m[2][2])/d,(m[0][1]*m[1][2]-m[0][2]*m[1][1])/d},
            {(m[1][2]*m[2][0]-m[1][0]*m[2][2])/d,(m[0][0]*m[2][2]-m[0][2]*m[2][0])/d,(m[0][2]*m[1][0]-m[0][0]*m[1][2])/d},
            {(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0])/d,(m[0][1]*m[2][0]-m[0][0]*m[2][1])/d,(m[0][0]*m[1][1]-m[0][1]*m[1][0])/d}}};
}

array<double,3> toEuler(M3 R){
    double ry=asin(max(-1.0,min(1.0,-R[2][0])));
    double cy=cos(ry),rx,rz;
    if(fabs(cy)>1e-7){rx=atan2(R[2][1]/cy,R[2][2]/cy);rz=atan2(R[1][0]/cy,R[0][0]/cy);}
    else{rx=0;rz=atan2(-R[0][1],R[1][1]);}
    return{rx,ry,rz};
}

M3 buildRot(double e,V3 t0,V3 t1,V3 t2,V3 t3){
    const double s3=sqrt(3.0),s6=sqrt(6.0);
    V3 v0={0,0,e*s6/4};
    V3 v1={0,e/s3,-e*s6/12};
    V3 v2={-e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    V3 v3={e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    V3 b1=vsub(v1,v0),b2=vsub(v2,v0),b3=vsub(v3,v0);
    M3 B={{{b1[0],b2[0],b3[0]},{b1[1],b2[1],b3[1]},{b1[2],b2[2],b3[2]}}};
    V3 a1=vsub(t1,t0),a2=vsub(t2,t0),a3=vsub(t3,t0);
    M3 A={{{a1[0],a2[0],a3[0]},{a1[1],a2[1],a3[1]},{a1[2],a2[2],a3[2]}}};
    return mmul(A,minv(B));
}

struct HS{V3 n;double d;};

vector<HS> buildHull(const vector<V3>& pts){
    int n=pts.size();
    V3 c={0,0,0};
    for(auto& p:pts){c[0]+=p[0];c[1]+=p[1];c[2]+=p[2];}
    c=vscl(1.0/n,c);
    vector<HS> hs;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    for(int j=i+1;j<n;j++)
    for(int k=j+1;k<n;k++){
        V3 nn=vnml(vcrs(vsub(pts[j],pts[i]),vsub(pts[k],pts[i])));
        if(vnrm(nn)<0.5) continue;
        double di=vdot(nn,pts[i]);
        bool ok=true;int s=0;
        for(int l=0;l<n&&ok;l++){
            if(l==i||l==j||l==k) continue;
            double v=vdot(nn,pts[l])-di;
            if(fabs(v)<1e-9) continue;
            int si=(v>0)?1:-1;
            if(!s) s=si; else if(s!=si) ok=false;
        }
        if(!ok) continue;
        if(vdot(nn,c)<di){nn=vscl(-1,nn);di=-di;}
        bool dup=false;
        for(auto& h:hs)
            if(fabs(vdot(h.n,nn)-1)<1e-6&&fabs(h.d-di)<1e-6){dup=true;break;}
        if(!dup) hs.push_back({nn,di});
    }
    return hs;
}

inline bool inHull(const vector<HS>& hs,const V3& p,double eps=1e-7){
    for(auto& h:hs)
        if(vdot(h.n,p)<h.d-eps) return false;
    return true;
}

// Fast output buffer
static char OBUF[1<<25];
static int OPOS=0;
void oflush(){fwrite(OBUF,1,OPOS,stdout);OPOS=0;}
void owrite(const char* s,int n){
    while(n>0){
        int space=(1<<25)-OPOS;
        if(space==0){oflush();space=1<<25;}
        int c=min(n,space);
        memcpy(OBUF+OPOS,s,c);
        OPOS+=c;s+=c;n-=c;
    }
}
void odbl(double x){char t[40];int n=sprintf(t,"%.10f",x);owrite(t,n);}
void oint(long long x){char t[32];int n=sprintf(t,"%lld",x);owrite(t,n);}
void ochar(char c){if(OPOS>=(1<<25))oflush();OBUF[OPOS++]=c;}

int main(){
    int V; double e;
    scanf("%d %lf",&V,&e);
    vector<V3> pts(V);
    for(int i=0;i<V;i++) scanf("%lf %lf %lf",&pts[i][0],&pts[i][1],&pts[i][2]);
    
    if(V<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    auto hs=buildHull(pts);
    if(hs.empty()){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    V3 lo={1e18,1e18,1e18},hi={-1e18,-1e18,-1e18};
    for(auto& p:pts)
        for(int d=0;d<3;d++){lo[d]=min(lo[d],p[d]);hi[d]=max(hi[d],p[d]);}
    
    const double S2=sqrt(2.0);
    double step=e/S2, r=step*0.5;
    
    // T1 centered: (-r,-r,-r),(r,r,-r),(r,-r,r),(-r,r,r)
    V3 C1[4]={{-r,-r,-r},{r,r,-r},{r,-r,r},{-r,r,r}};
    // T2 centered: (-r,-r,r),(r,r,r),(r,-r,-r),(-r,r,-r) [swap C2[2],C2[3] for buildRot to get det=+1]
    V3 C2[4]={{-r,-r,r},{r,r,r},{r,-r,-r},{-r,r,-r}};
    
    M3 R1=buildRot(e,C1[0],C1[1],C1[2],C1[3]);
    M3 R2=buildRot(e,C2[0],C2[1],C2[3],C2[2]); // note: C2[3] before C2[2]
    
    auto eu1=toEuler(R1);
    auto eu2=toEuler(R2);
    
    int umin=(int)floor(lo[0]/step)-2, umax=(int)ceil(hi[0]/step)+2;
    int vmin=(int)floor(lo[1]/step)-2, vmax=(int)ceil(hi[1]/step)+2;
    int wmin=(int)floor(lo[2]/step)-2, wmax=(int)ceil(hi[2]/step)+2;
    
    // Two-pass approach
    long long cnt=0;
    
    for(int u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(int v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(int w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1) continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                V3 p00={qu,qv,qw};
                V3 p01={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
                // T1: p00, p01, (qu+step,qv,qw+step), (qu,qv+step,qw+step)
                {
                    V3 p2={qu+step,qv,qw+step}, p3={qu,qv+step,qw+step};
                    if(inHull(hs,p00)&&inHull(hs,p01)&&inHull(hs,p2)&&inHull(hs,p3)) cnt++;
                }
                // T2: p00, p01, (qu+step,qv,qw-step), (qu,qv+step,qw-step)
                {
                    V3 p2={qu+step,qv,qw-step}, p3={qu,qv+step,qw-step};
                    if(inHull(hs,p00)&&inHull(hs,p01)&&inHull(hs,p2)&&inHull(hs,p3)) cnt++;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    oint(cnt); ochar('\n');
    
    for(int u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(int v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(int w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1) continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                V3 p00={qu,qv,qw};
                V3 p01={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
                // T1
                {
                    V3 p2={qu+step,qv,qw+step}, p3={qu,qv+step,qw+step};
                    if(inHull(hs,p00)&&inHull(hs,p01)&&inHull(hs,p2)&&inHull(hs,p3)){
                        odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw+r);ochar(' ');
                        odbl(eu1[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[2]);ochar('\n');
                    }
                }
                // T2
                {
                    V3 p2={qu+step,qv,qw-step}, p3={qu,qv+step,qw-step};
                    if(inHull(hs,p00)&&inHull(hs,p01)&&inHull(hs,p2)&&inHull(hs,p3)){
                        odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw-r);ochar(' ');
                        odbl(eu2[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[2]);ochar('\n');
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    oflush();
    return 0;
}
```

This should work. Let me do one final check of the inHull and buildHull functions.

buildHull: for each triple (i,j,k), compute normal to the plane. If all other points are on the same side, it's a hull face. Make normal point inward (toward centroid). Add to hs.

Wait, I said "point toward centroid" means `dot(nn, cen) > di`. After the flip: `dot(nn, cen) >= di`. And "inside" means `dot(nn, p) >= di - eps` for each plane.

Let me trace through:
- Initial: `nn` is normalized normal, `di = dot(nn, pts[i])`.
- `dot(nn, cen) < di` → centroid is on the side where dot<di, meaning the "inside" is on that side.
- Wait: if `dot(nn, cen) < di`, the centroid is "below" the plane (dot < di), which means the interior is below the plane.
- After flip: `nn = -nn, di = -di`. Now `dot(-nn, cen) = -dot(nn,cen) > -di` → `dot(nn', cen) > di'` where nn'=-nn, di'=-di.
- Inside = `dot(nn', p) >= di' - eps`.

Hmm, let me verify with a simple example. Say the plane is z=1 (nn=(0,0,1), di=1), and centroid at z=0.5.
dot(nn, cen) = 0.5 < 1 = di. So we flip: nn'=(0,0,-1), di'=-1.
Inside = dot((0,0,-1), p) >= -1 - eps = z ≥ 1 - eps for z being the third coordinate of p.

But that's the OPPOSITE of what I want! If centroid is at z=0.5 and the hull plane is z=1, then "inside" should be z ≤ 1 (below the plane).

Wait, I think I have the sign convention wrong. Let me re-examine.

Actually: for a convex hull, a point P is inside iff for each face plane, P is on the same side as the centroid (which is guaranteed to be inside).

For plane: n·x = d (where n is some normal and d is offset).
Centroid satisfies: n·cen = d + delta (for some delta, positive or negative).
If delta > 0: centroid is on the "+" side (n·x > d). Inside = n·x > d (well, ≥ d - eps for numerical tolerance).
If delta < 0: centroid is on the "-" side. Inside = n·x < d.

For implementation: I want to normalize so that "inside" always means n·x ≥ d.
So if delta < 0 (centroid on "-" side), flip normal: n → -n, d → -d.
Then new delta = -n·cen - (-d) = d - n·cen = |delta| > 0. ✓

In my code: `if(dot(nn,c)<di){nn=vscl(-1,nn);di=-di;}`
This flips when `dot(nn,c) < di`, i.e., centroid on "-" side. After flip: `dot(-nn,c) = -dot(nn,c) > -di = di'`. ✓

Inside check: `dot(h.n, p) >= h.d - eps`. With the flipped normal, this is correct. ✓

Let me verify with the example:
Plane z=1: nn=(0,0,1), di=1. Centroid at z=0.5.
dot(nn,cen) = 0.5 < 1 = di → flip: nn'=(0,0,-1), di'=-1.
Inside check: dot((0,0,-1),p) >= -1 - eps → -pz >= -1 - eps → pz <= 1 + eps. ✓ (inside the hull, below z=1)

For a point at z=0: dot((0,0,-1),(0,0,0)) = 0 >= -1 - eps ✓ (inside).
For a point at z=2: dot((0,0,-1),(0,0,2)) = -2 < -1 - eps (approximately -1) → ✗ (outside). ✓

Great, the convention is correct!

Now let me also check: the initial normal direction for the triple (pts[i], pts[j], pts[k]).
normal = cross(pts[j]-pts[i], pts[k]-pts[i]).

This normal can point in either direction. After normalization, we check which side the centroid is on and flip if needed. ✓

One more edge case: if ALL other points are coplanar (the triple is at the boundary of all points, like 3 out of 4 vertices of a tetrahedron), then `side = 0` after the loop, meaning `ok=true` and the plane is added. Is this correct?

For a regular tetrahedron with 4 vertices, each triple of 3 vertices forms a face, and the 4th vertex is on one side. After the check, `side` would be set to 1 or -1 by the 4th point. ✓

For a degenerate case where all 4 points are coplanar (2D polyhedron), all triples would have `side=0` (no points not coplanar). These would be added as half-spaces, but they might be inconsistent. The containment check would then fail (any point would be on both sides). This is a degenerate case we handle by returning 0 tets.

For well-formed 3D polyhedra (V≥4, not degenerate), the hull is computed correctly.

I'm satisfied with the implementation. Let me write the absolute final version now.

Actually, let me reconsider one thing. I need to also handle the case where V>=4 but all V points are coplanar (degenerate 2D "polyhedron"). In this case, the convex hull would have faces that are contradictory (the normal and its negative would both be "inside" directions). The `buildHull` function might add both, resulting in `hs` being inconsistent.

To handle: after computing hs, check if any two half-spaces are contradictory (n1 = -n2, d1 = -d2 + something). If so, the "container" is degenerate and we output 0.

But this is an edge case the problem might not test. Let me add a simple volume check:
If the bounding box volume is 0 or the hull has fewer than 4 half-spaces, output 0.

Actually: a valid 3D convex polyhedron has at least 4 faces (for a tetrahedron). If `hs.size() < 4`, the container is degenerate.

```cpp
if(hs.size()<4){puts("0");return 0;}
```

Let me add this.

Also: I should check that the FCC lattice enumeration makes sense for very small containers (e.g., smaller than one tetrahedron). In that case, the loop might find 0 valid tets, which is correct.

One more thing: for the `(u+v+w)&1` check with negative values in two's complement:
In two's complement (standard for modern CPUs and C++), `-1 = 0xFFFF...F`, so `(-1)&1 = 1` (odd ✓).
`-2 = 0xFFFF...E`, so `(-2)&1 = 0` (even ✓).
This works correctly for parity checking in two's complement. ✓

OK I'm ready to write the final code. Here it is. This is THE final version:

```cpp
#include <cstdio>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <array>
#include <algorithm>
#include <cstring>

using namespace std;
typedef array<double,3> V3;
typedef array<array<double,3>,3> M3;

// --- Vector math ---
V3 vadd(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]+b[0],a[1]+b[1],a[2]+b[2]};}
V3 vsub(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]-b[0],a[1]-b[1],a[2]-b[2]};}
V3 vscl(double s,V3 a){return{s*a[0],s*a[1],s*a[2]};}
double vdot(V3 a,V3 b){return a[0]*b[0]+a[1]*b[1]+a[2]*b[2];}
V3 vcrs(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[1]*b[2]-a[2]*b[1],a[2]*b[0]-a[0]*b[2],a[0]*b[1]-a[1]*b[0]};}
double vnrm(V3 a){return sqrt(vdot(a,a));}
V3 vnml(V3 a){double n=vnrm(a);return n<1e-14?V3{0,0,0}:vscl(1/n,a);}

// --- Matrix math ---
M3 mmul(M3 a,M3 b){
    M3 r{};
    for(int i=0;i<3;i++)for(int j=0;j<3;j++)for(int k=0;k<3;k++)
        r[i][j]+=a[i][k]*b[k][j];
    return r;
}
double mdet(M3 m){
    return m[0][0]*(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])
          -m[0][1]*(m[1][0]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][0])
          +m[0][2]*(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0]);
}
M3 minv(M3 m){
    double d=mdet(m);
    return{{{(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])/d,
             (m[0][2]*m[2][1]-m[0][1]*m[2][2])/d,
             (m[0][1]*m[1][2]-m[0][2]*m[1][1])/d},
            {(m[1][2]*m[2][0]-m[1][0]*m[2][2])/d,
             (m[0][0]*m[2][2]-m[0][2]*m[2][0])/d,
             (m[0][2]*m[1][0]-m[0][0]*m[1][2])/d},
            {(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0])/d,
             (m[0][1]*m[2][0]-m[0][0]*m[2][1])/d,
             (m[0][0]*m[1][1]-m[0][1]*m[1][0])/d}}};
}

// --- Euler angles (ZYX: R = Rz*Ry*Rx) from rotation matrix ---
array<double,3> matToEuler(M3 R){
    double ry=asin(max(-1.0,min(1.0,-R[2][0])));
    double cy=cos(ry),rx,rz;
    if(fabs(cy)>1e-7){
        rx=atan2(R[2][1]/cy,R[2][2]/cy);
        rz=atan2(R[1][0]/cy,R[0][0]/cy);
    }else{
        rx=0;
        rz=atan2(-R[0][1],R[1][1]);
    }
    return{rx,ry,rz};
}

// Build rotation matrix mapping canonical tet → target tet
// Canonical (centered at origin, edge e):
//   v0=(0,0,e*sqrt(6)/4), v1=(0,e/sqrt(3),-e*sqrt(6)/12),
//   v2=(-e/2,-e/(2*sqrt(3)),-e*sqrt(6)/12), v3=(e/2,-e/(2*sqrt(3)),-e*sqrt(6)/12)
// Returns R such that R*vi_canonical = ti_target
M3 buildRot(double e,V3 t0,V3 t1,V3 t2,V3 t3){
    const double s3=sqrt(3.0),s6=sqrt(6.0);
    V3 v0={0,0,e*s6/4};
    V3 v1={0,e/s3,-e*s6/12};
    V3 v2={-e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    V3 v3={e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    // B: edge matrix of canonical (columns = v1-v0, v2-v0, v3-v0)
    V3 b1=vsub(v1,v0),b2=vsub(v2,v0),b3=vsub(v3,v0);
    M3 B={{{b1[0],b2[0],b3[0]},{b1[1],b2[1],b3[1]},{b1[2],b2[2],b3[2]}}};
    // A: edge matrix of target (columns = t1-t0, t2-t0, t3-t0)
    V3 a1=vsub(t1,t0),a2=vsub(t2,t0),a3=vsub(t3,t0);
    M3 A={{{a1[0],a2[0],a3[0]},{a1[1],a2[1],a3[1]},{a1[2],a2[2],a3[2]}}};
    // R = A * B^{-1}
    return mmul(A,minv(B));
}

// Half-space: dot(n,p) >= d means inside
struct HS{V3 n;double d;};

vector<HS> buildHull(const vector<V3>& pts){
    int n=pts.size();
    // Centroid
    V3 cen={0,0,0};
    for(auto& p:pts){cen[0]+=p[0];cen[1]+=p[1];cen[2]+=p[2];}
    cen=vscl(1.0/n,cen);
    
    vector<HS> hs;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    for(int j=i+1;j<n;j++)
    for(int k=j+1;k<n;k++){
        V3 nn=vnml(vcrs(vsub(pts[j],pts[i]),vsub(pts[k],pts[i])));
        if(vnrm(nn)<0.5) continue; // degenerate triple
        double di=vdot(nn,pts[i]);
        // Check all other points on same side
        bool ok=true;
        int side=0;
        for(int l=0;l<n&&ok;l++){
            if(l==i||l==j||l==k) continue;
            double v=vdot(nn,pts[l])-di;
            if(fabs(v)<1e-9) continue; // coplanar
            int s=(v>0)?1:-1;
            if(!side) side=s;
            else if(s!=side) ok=false;
        }
        if(!ok) continue;
        // Ensure normal points inward (toward centroid)
        if(vdot(nn,cen)<di){nn=vscl(-1,nn);di=-di;}
        // Deduplicate
        bool dup=false;
        for(auto& h:hs)
            if(fabs(vdot(h.n,nn)-1)<1e-6&&fabs(h.d-di)<1e-6){dup=true;break;}
        if(!dup) hs.push_back({nn,di});
    }
    return hs;
}

inline bool inHull(const vector<HS>& hs,const V3& p,double eps=1e-7){
    for(const auto& h:hs)
        if(vdot(h.n,p)<h.d-eps) return false;
    return true;
}

// Fast output
static char OBUF[1<<26]; // 64MB
static int OPOS=0;
void oflush(){fwrite(OBUF,1,OPOS,stdout);OPOS=0;}
void owrite(const char* s,int n){
    if(OPOS+n>(1<<26)){oflush();}
    memcpy(OBUF+OPOS,s,n);
    OPOS+=n;
}
void ochar(char c){if(OPOS>=(1<<26))oflush();OBUF[OPOS++]=c;}
void odbl(double x){char t[40];owrite(t,sprintf(t,"%.10f",x));}
void oint(long long x){char t[32];owrite(t,sprintf(t,"%lld",x));}

int main(){
    int V; double e;
    scanf("%d %lf",&V,&e);
    
    vector<V3> pts(V);
    for(int i=0;i<V;i++) scanf("%lf %lf %lf",&pts[i][0],&pts[i][1],&pts[i][2]);
    
    if(V<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    vector<HS> hs=buildHull(pts);
    if(hs.size()<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    // Bounding box
    V3 lo={1e18,1e18,1e18},hi={-1e18,-1e18,-1e18};
    for(auto& p:pts)
        for(int d=0;d<3;d++){lo[d]=min(lo[d],p[d]);hi[d]=max(hi[d],p[d]);}
    
    // FCC lattice: step = e/sqrt(2), r = step/2 = e/(2*sqrt(2))
    const double S2=sqrt(2.0);
    double step=e/S2, r=step*0.5;
    
    // T1 centered vertices (edge e): {(-r,-r,-r),(r,r,-r),(r,-r,r),(-r,r,r)}
    // T2 centered vertices (edge e): {(-r,-r,r),(r,r,r),(r,-r,-r),(-r,r,-r)}
    V3 C1[4]={{-r,-r,-r},{r,r,-r},{r,-r,r},{-r,r,r}};
    V3 C2[4]={{-r,-r,r},{r,r,r},{r,-r,-r},{-r,r,-r}};
    
    // Build rotation matrices
    // For T1: det(A)/det(B) > 0 → proper rotation
    M3 R1=buildRot(e,C1[0],C1[1],C1[2],C1[3]);
    // For T2: need to swap C2[2],C2[3] to get proper rotation (det > 0)
    M3 R2=buildRot(e,C2[0],C2[1],C2[3],C2[2]);
    
    auto eu1=matToEuler(R1);
    auto eu2=matToEuler(R2);
    
    // Lattice bounds
    int umin=(int)floor(lo[0]/step)-2, umax=(int)ceil(hi[0]/step)+2;
    int vmin=(int)floor(lo[1]/step)-2, vmax=(int)ceil(hi[1]/step)+2;
    int wmin=(int)floor(lo[2]/step)-2, wmax=(int)ceil(hi[2]/step)+2;
    
    // Pass 1: count
    long long cnt=0;
    for(int u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(int v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(int w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1) continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                // T1: Q,(u+1,v+1,w),(u+1,v,w+1),(u,v+1,w+1) scaled by step
                if(inHull(hs,{qu,qv,qw})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu+step,qv+step,qw})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu+step,qv,qw+step})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu,qv+step,qw+step})) cnt++;
                // T2: Q,(u+1,v+1,w),(u+1,v,w-1),(u,v+1,w-1)
                if(inHull(hs,{qu,qv,qw})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu+step,qv+step,qw})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu+step,qv,qw-step})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu,qv+step,qw-step})) cnt++;
            }
        }
    }
    
    oint(cnt); ochar('\n');
    
    // Pass 2: output
    for(int u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(int v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(int w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1) continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                // T1
                if(inHull(hs,{qu,qv,qw})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu+step,qv+step,qw})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu+step,qv,qw+step})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu,qv+step,qw+step})){
                    odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw+r);ochar(' ');
                    odbl(eu1[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[2]);ochar('\n');
                }
                // T2
                if(inHull(hs,{qu,qv,qw})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu+step,qv+step,qw})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu+step,qv,qw-step})&&
                   inHull(hs,{qu,qv+step,qw-step})){
                    odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw-r);ochar(' ');
                    odbl(eu2[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[2]);ochar('\n');
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    oflush();
    return 0;
}
```

Wait, in the code above I use `{qu,qv,qw}` as a V3 initializer. In C++17/20 this should work with `std::array<double,3>` since it's an aggregate. Let me verify:
`V3 p = {qu, qv, qw};` ✓ This is valid for `array<double,3>`.
And `inHull(hs, {qu,qv,qw})` passes a temporary V3 initialized with those values. ✓

But wait, `inHull` takes `const V3& p`. Can I pass a brace-initializer as a const reference? In C++11 and later, yes, for aggregate types. And with `const auto&` or explicit type, it should work. Let me make it explicit:
```cpp
inHull(hs, V3{qu,qv,qw})
```
This is safer and more explicit.

Actually, let me check: `void f(const V3& x){}; f({1,2,3});` - is this valid in C++?
In C++11+: yes, you can pass a braced initializer as a const reference to an aggregate type. The compiler creates a temporary V3{1,2,3} and binds it. ✓

OK the code should compile. Let me just use `V3{...}` explicitly to be safe.

Also: I should double-check that `inHull` takes a const reference to `V3`. Current signature: `inline bool inHull(const vector<HS>& hs,const V3& p,double eps=1e-7)`. ✓

Let me also make sure the output buffer check is correct in `owrite`:
```cpp
void owrite(const char* s,int n){
    if(OPOS+n>(1<<26)){oflush();}
    memcpy(OBUF+OPOS,s,n);
    OPOS+=n;
}
```
This checks if OPOS+n would overflow the buffer. If it would, flush first. Then write. But what if n > (1<<26)? This would overflow even after flush! Let me handle that:
```cpp
void owrite(const char* s,int n){
    while(n>0){
        if(OPOS>=(1<<26)) oflush();
        int cap=(1<<26)-OPOS;
        int c=min(n,cap);
        memcpy(OBUF+OPOS,s,c);
        OPOS+=c; s+=c; n-=c;
    }
}
```
For small writes (like a double ≈ 15 chars), the single-if version is fine. But to be safe, use the while loop.

Actually, for `odbl`, n ≤ 40 << (1<<26), so it's fine.

Let me finalize. Here's the TRULY final code:

I realize I should also double-check the output format. The problem says:
"Line 1: K (number of tetrahedrons placed)"
"Lines 2..K+1: cx cy cz rx ry rz (center + Euler angles in radians)"

My output: first line is K, then K lines with 6 doubles each. ✓

One more thing: precision. I'm using `"%.10f"` for 10 decimal places. This gives coordinates accurate to 0.1 nanometers for sizes up to 100m, which should be more than enough.

For the Euler angles: `%.10f` gives 10 decimal places in radians, accurate to ~10^-10 rad ≈ 10^-8 degrees. More than sufficient.

Let me write the FINAL FINAL code now. I'll clean it up one last time and that's it.

Here's what I want to verify one more time: The `buildRot` function for T2 with the swapped arguments `buildRot(e, C2[0], C2[1], C2[3], C2[2])`.

This computes R2 such that:
- R2 * v0c = C2[0] = (-r,-r,r)
- R2 * v1c = C2[1] = (r,r,r)
- R2 * v2c = C2[3] = (-r,r,-r)  ← note: C2[3] is the THIRD argument
- R2 * v3c = C2[2] = (r,-r,-r)  ← note: C2[2] is the FOURTH argument

So the checker would reconstruct:
- vertex corresponding to v0c → C2[0] + center = center + (-r,-r,r)
- vertex corresponding to v1c → C2[1] + center = center + (r,r,r)
- vertex corresponding to v2c → C2[3] + center = center + (-r,r,-r)
- vertex corresponding to v3c → C2[2] + center = center + (r,-r,-r)

As a SET: {center+(-r,-r,r), center+(r,r,r), center+(-r,r,-r), center+(r,-r,-r)} = T2 vertices relative to center. ✓

The actual T2 tet vertices (from the loop):
p0 = (qu, qv, qw) = center - (r,r,-r) + (0,0,0) = ... wait:
center = (qu+r, qv+r, qw-r)
p0 = (qu, qv, qw) = center + (-r,-r,r) ← wait: center + (-r,-r,r) = (qu+r-r, qv+r-r, qw-r+r) = (qu, qv, qw) ✓
p1 = (qu+step, qv+step, qw) = center + (step-r, step-r, r) = center + (r,r,r) ✓ (since step-r = r)
p2 = (qu+step, qv, qw-step) = center + (r,-r,-step-(-r)) ... let me compute:
center+(r,-r,-r) = (qu+r+r, qv+r-r, qw-r-r) = (qu+2r, qv, qw-2r) = (qu+step, qv, qw-step) ✓
p3 = (qu, qv+step, qw-step) = center+(-r,r,-r) = (qu+r-r, qv+r+r, qw-r-r) = (qu, qv+step, qw-step) ✓

And the checker would reconstruct these 4 points in the SET {C2[0],C2[1],C2[2],C2[3]} + center:
{(-r,-r,r),(r,r,r),(r,-r,-r),(-r,r,-r)} + center = {p0,p1,p2,p3} ✓

Wait: I said the checker maps:
- v0c → C2[0] = (-r,-r,r) → center + (-r,-r,r) = p0 ✓
- v1c → C2[1] = (r,r,r) → center + (r,r,r) = p1 ✓
- v2c → C2[3] = (-r,r,-r) → center + (-r,r,-r) = p3 ✓
- v3c → C2[2] = (r,-r,-r) → center + (r,-r,-r) = p2 ✓

So the checker gets {p0,p1,p2,p3} = same 4 vertex positions. ✓ Correct.

The checker verifies:
1. All 4 points inside hull ✓ (we verified this in our loop)
2. No overlaps (guaranteed by honeycomb structure) ✓

I'm confident the code is correct. Let me write the complete final version now.

Ah wait, I just realized there might be an issue with very large integer indices. If `umin`, `umax`, etc. are very large (like 10^9 for a "ludicrous scale" container with e=1), then `int` might overflow.

For a container of linear size L and edge e:
umin ≈ -L*√2/e, umax ≈ L*√2/e
For L=10^6, e=1: umin≈-1.4×10^6, umax≈1.4×10^6. Fine for int (max ~2.1×10^9).
For L=10^9, e=1: umin≈-1.4×10^9. Near int limit! Use long long for safety.

Let me use `long long` for u, v, w:

```cpp
long long umin=(long long)floor(lo[0]/step)-2, umax=(long long)ceil(hi[0]/step)+2;
// ...
for(long long u=umin; u<=umax; u++) {
    // ...
}
```

But then `(u+v+w)&1` uses long long, which is fine.
And `double qu = u*step;` might lose precision for very large u. But for u=10^9 and step=1/√2≈0.707, qu ≈ 7×10^8, which is representable in double (since double has 53 bits of mantissa ≈ 9×10^15, much larger than 7×10^8). ✓

Let me use long long for the loop indices.

Also: `(long long)(umax-umin+1)*(vmax-vmin+1)*(wmax-wmin+1)` might overflow if each dimension has ~10^6 points. 10^6^3 = 10^18, which overflows long long (max ~9.2×10^18). But for this problem, a "ludicrous" container is unlikely to have 10^18 lattice points.

For safety, I could add a check and bail early if the container is too large:
```cpp
long long est = (umax-umin+1) * (long long)(vmax-vmin+1) * (wmax-wmin+1);
if(est > 1LL<<40) { /* too large, limit somehow */ }
```

For now, let me just trust the problem won't have containers requiring 10^9+ lattice points in each dimension.

Let me write the final code. I'll use long long for indices and add some safety.

OK HERE IS THE TRULY FINAL CODE (no more deliberating):

```cpp
#include <cstdio>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <array>
#include <algorithm>
#include <cstring>

using namespace std;
typedef array<double,3> V3;
typedef array<array<double,3>,3> M3;

V3 vadd(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]+b[0],a[1]+b[1],a[2]+b[2]};}
V3 vsub(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]-b[0],a[1]-b[1],a[2]-b[2]};}
V3 vscl(double s,V3 a){return{s*a[0],s*a[1],s*a[2]};}
double vdot(V3 a,V3 b){return a[0]*b[0]+a[1]*b[1]+a[2]*b[2];}
V3 vcrs(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[1]*b[2]-a[2]*b[1],a[2]*b[0]-a[0]*b[2],a[0]*b[1]-a[1]*b[0]};}
double vnrm(V3 a){return sqrt(vdot(a,a));}
V3 vnml(V3 a){double n=vnrm(a);return n<1e-14?V3{0,0,0}:vscl(1/n,a);}

M3 mmul(M3 a,M3 b){M3 r{};for(int i=0;i<3;i++)for(int j=0;j<3;j++)for(int k=0;k<3;k++)r[i][j]+=a[i][k]*b[k][j];return r;}
double mdet(M3 m){return m[0][0]*(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])-m[0][1]*(m[1][0]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][0])+m[0][2]*(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0]);}
M3 minv(M3 m){
    double d=mdet(m);
    return{{{(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])/d,(m[0][2]*m[2][1]-m[0][1]*m[2][2])/d,(m[0][1]*m[1][2]-m[0][2]*m[1][1])/d},
            {(m[1][2]*m[2][0]-m[1][0]*m[2][2])/d,(m[0][0]*m[2][2]-m[0][2]*m[2][0])/d,(m[0][2]*m[1][0]-m[0][0]*m[1][2])/d},
            {(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0])/d,(m[0][1]*m[2][0]-m[0][0]*m[2][1])/d,(m[0][0]*m[1][1]-m[0][1]*m[1][0])/d}}};
}

array<double,3> matToEuler(M3 R){
    double ry=asin(max(-1.0,min(1.0,-R[2][0])));
    double cy=cos(ry),rx,rz;
    if(fabs(cy)>1e-7){rx=atan2(R[2][1]/cy,R[2][2]/cy);rz=atan2(R[1][0]/cy,R[0][0]/cy);}
    else{rx=0;rz=atan2(-R[0][1],R[1][1]);}
    return{rx,ry,rz};
}

M3 buildRot(double e,V3 t0,V3 t1,V3 t2,V3 t3){
    const double s3=sqrt(3.0),s6=sqrt(6.0);
    V3 v0={0,0,e*s6/4},v1={0,e/s3,-e*s6/12},v2={-e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12},v3={e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    V3 b1=vsub(v1,v0),b2=vsub(v2,v0),b3=vsub(v3,v0);
    M3 B={{{b1[0],b2[0],b3[0]},{b1[1],b2[1],b3[1]},{b1[2],b2[2],b3[2]}}};
    V3 a1=vsub(t1,t0),a2=vsub(t2,t0),a3=vsub(t3,t0);
    M3 A={{{a1[0],a2[0],a3[0]},{a1[1],a2[1],a3[1]},{a1[2],a2[2],a3[2]}}};
    return mmul(A,minv(B));
}

struct HS{V3 n;double d;};

vector<HS> buildHull(const vector<V3>& pts){
    int n=pts.size();
    V3 cen={0,0,0};
    for(auto& p:pts){cen[0]+=p[0];cen[1]+=p[1];cen[2]+=p[2];}
    cen=vscl(1.0/n,cen);
    vector<HS> hs;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    for(int j=i+1;j<n;j++)
    for(int k=j+1;k<n;k++){
        V3 nn=vnml(vcrs(vsub(pts[j],pts[i]),vsub(pts[k],pts[i])));
        if(vnrm(nn)<0.5)continue;
        double di=vdot(nn,pts[i]);
        bool ok=true;int s=0;
        for(int l=0;l<n&&ok;l++){
            if(l==i||l==j||l==k)continue;
            double v=vdot(nn,pts[l])-di;
            if(fabs(v)<1e-9)continue;
            int si=(v>0)?1:-1;
            if(!s)s=si;else if(s!=si)ok=false;
        }
        if(!ok)continue;
        if(vdot(nn,cen)<di){nn=vscl(-1,nn);di=-di;}
        bool dup=false;
        for(auto& h:hs)if(fabs(vdot(h.n,nn)-1)<1e-6&&fabs(h.d-di)<1e-6){dup=true;break;}
        if(!dup)hs.push_back({nn,di});
    }
    return hs;
}

inline bool inHull(const vector<HS>& hs,V3 p,double eps=1e-7){
    for(const auto& h:hs)if(vdot(h.n,p)<h.d-eps)return false;
    return true;
}

static char OB[1<<26];
static int OP=0;
void oflush(){fwrite(OB,1,OP,stdout);OP=0;}
void ochar(char c){if(OP>=(1<<26))oflush();OB[OP++]=c;}
void odbl(double x){char t[40];int n=sprintf(t,"%.10f",x);if(OP+n>=(1<<26))oflush();memcpy(OB+OP,t,n);OP+=n;}
void oint(long long x){char t[32];int n=sprintf(t,"%lld",x);if(OP+n>=(1<<26))oflush();memcpy(OB+OP,t,n);OP+=n;}

int main(){
    int V;double e;
    scanf("%d %lf",&V,&e);
    vector<V3> pts(V);
    for(int i=0;i<V;i++)scanf("%lf %lf %lf",&pts[i][0],&pts[i][1],&pts[i][2]);
    
    if(V<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    auto hs=buildHull(pts);
    if((int)hs.size()<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    V3 lo={1e18,1e18,1e18},hi={-1e18,-1e18,-1e18};
    for(auto& p:pts)for(int d=0;d<3;d++){lo[d]=min(lo[d],p[d]);hi[d]=max(hi[d],p[d]);}
    
    const double S2=sqrt(2.0);
    double step=e/S2,r=step*0.5;
    
    V3 C1[4]={{-r,-r,-r},{r,r,-r},{r,-r,r},{-r,r,r}};
    V3 C2[4]={{-r,-r,r},{r,r,r},{r,-r,-r},{-r,r,-r}};
    M3 R1=buildRot(e,C1[0],C1[1],C1[2],C1[3]);
    M3 R2=buildRot(e,C2[0],C2[1],C2[3],C2[2]);
    auto eu1=matToEuler(R1);
    auto eu2=matToEuler(R2);
    
    long long umin=(long long)floor(lo[0]/step)-2,umax=(long long)ceil(hi[0]/step)+2;
    long long vmin=(long long)floor(lo[1]/step)-2,vmax=(long long)ceil(hi[1]/step)+2;
    long long wmin=(long long)floor(lo[2]/step)-2,wmax=(long long)ceil(hi[2]/step)+2;
    
    // Pass 1: count
    long long cnt=0;
    for(long long u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(long long v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(long long w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1LL)continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                if(inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv,qw})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv+step,qw})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw+step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw+step}))cnt++;
                if(inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv,qw})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv+step,qw})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw-step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw-step}))cnt++;
            }
        }
    }
    
    oint(cnt);ochar('\n');
    
    // Pass 2: output
    for(long long u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(long long v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(long long w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1LL)continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                if(inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv,qw})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv+step,qw})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw+step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw+step})){
                    odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw+r);ochar(' ');
                    odbl(eu1[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[2]);ochar('\n');
                }
                if(inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv,qw})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv+step,qw})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw-step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw-step})){
                    odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw-r);ochar(' ');
                    odbl(eu2[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[2]);ochar('\n');
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    oflush();
    return 0;
}
```

This is the final code. Let me do a final review:

1. Parsing: ✓ (scanf for V, e, then coordinates)
2. Degenerate case V<4: ✓ (output 0)
3. Hull building: ✓ (O(n^4) algorithm)
4. Hull with <4 faces: ✓ (output 0, degenerate container)
5. Bounding box: ✓
6. FCC lattice step: ✓ (e/√2)
7. T1 and T2 centered vertices: ✓ (verified analytically)
8. Rotation matrices: ✓ (buildRot with proper swap for T2)
9. Euler angles: ✓ (ZYX convention)
10. Two-pass enumeration: ✓
11. Output format: ✓ (K then K lines of cx cy cz rx ry rz)
12. Fast output buffer: ✓

I'm satisfied with this. Let me now write this as my final answer.

Actually, one small thing: `(u+v+w)&1LL` - when u,v,w are `long long`, `u+v+w` is `long long`, and `&1LL` is correct. ✓

Also: for the inner T1 check, I repeat `inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv,qw})` twice (once for T1, once for T2). This is redundant but harmless - just a minor inefficiency. I could cache it:

```cpp
bool base_in = inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv,qw});
if(base_in && ...) cnt++; // T1
if(base_in && ...) cnt++; // T2
```

Let me add this optimization.

Also, T1 and T2 share two vertices: Q=(qu,qv,qw) and Q+A=(qu+step,qv+step,qw). So cache these:

```cpp
bool p0_in = inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv,qw});
bool p1_in = inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv+step,qw});
// T1
if(p0_in&&p1_in&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw+step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw+step}))cnt++;
// T2
if(p0_in&&p1_in&&inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw-step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw-step}))cnt++;
```

This halves the number of hull checks (since p0 and p1 are checked once instead of twice). Good optimization.

Let me add this to both the count and output passes.

For the output pass, I also need to handle the "early out" correctly. If p0_in is false, skip both T1 and T2.

Here's the optimized version of the inner loop:

```cpp
bool p0=inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv,qw});
if(!p0) continue; // Both T1 and T2 need Q
bool p1=inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv+step,qw});
if(!p1) continue; // Both need Q+A
// T1
if(inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw+step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw+step})){
    cnt++; // or output
}
// T2
if(inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw-step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw-step})){
    cnt++; // or output
}
```

Wait but the `continue` would skip both T1 and T2 for this (u,v,w). That's correct! If Q or Q+A is outside, neither T1 nor T2 can be valid. ✓

This optimization reduces unnecessary hull checks and also enables early termination via `continue`.

Let me incorporate this. Here's the optimized inner body:

For the count pass:
```cpp
for(long long w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
    if((u+v+w)&1LL)continue;
    double qw=w*step;
    V3 p0={qu,qv,qw};
    V3 p1={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
    if(!inHull(hs,p0)||!inHull(hs,p1))continue;
    if(inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw+step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw+step}))cnt++;
    if(inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw-step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw-step}))cnt++;
}
```

This is cleaner. Let me use this pattern.

Actually hmm: if the container contains many tets, the `continue` won't help much (most p0 and p1 will be inside). But for boundary cases (many lattice points near the boundary where p0 or p1 is outside), this helps.

For the output pass: use the same optimization.

Let me write the truly final code now. NO MORE DELIBERATING.

```cpp
#include <cstdio>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <array>
#include <algorithm>
#include <cstring>

using namespace std;
typedef array<double,3> V3;
typedef array<array<double,3>,3> M3;

V3 vadd(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]+b[0],a[1]+b[1],a[2]+b[2]};}
V3 vsub(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]-b[0],a[1]-b[1],a[2]-b[2]};}
V3 vscl(double s,V3 a){return{s*a[0],s*a[1],s*a[2]};}
double vdot(V3 a,V3 b){return a[0]*b[0]+a[1]*b[1]+a[2]*b[2];}
V3 vcrs(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[1]*b[2]-a[2]*b[1],a[2]*b[0]-a[0]*b[2],a[0]*b[1]-a[1]*b[0]};}
double vnrm(V3 a){return sqrt(vdot(a,a));}
V3 vnml(V3 a){double n=vnrm(a);return n<1e-14?V3{0,0,0}:vscl(1/n,a);}

M3 mmul(M3 a,M3 b){M3 r{};for(int i=0;i<3;i++)for(int j=0;j<3;j++)for(int k=0;k<3;k++)r[i][j]+=a[i][k]*b[k][j];return r;}
double mdet(M3 m){return m[0][0]*(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])-m[0][1]*(m[1][0]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][0])+m[0][2]*(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0]);}
M3 minv(M3 m){
    double d=mdet(m);
    return{{{(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])/d,(m[0][2]*m[2][1]-m[0][1]*m[2][2])/d,(m[0][1]*m[1][2]-m[0][2]*m[1][1])/d},
            {(m[1][2]*m[2][0]-m[1][0]*m[2][2])/d,(m[0][0]*m[2][2]-m[0][2]*m[2][0])/d,(m[0][2]*m[1][0]-m[0][0]*m[1][2])/d},
            {(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0])/d,(m[0][1]*m[2][0]-m[0][0]*m[2][1])/d,(m[0][0]*m[1][1]-m[0][1]*m[1][0])/d}}};
}

// ZYX Euler: R = Rz*Ry*Rx
array<double,3> matToEuler(M3 R){
    double ry=asin(max(-1.0,min(1.0,-R[2][0])));
    double cy=cos(ry),rx,rz;
    if(fabs(cy)>1e-7){rx=atan2(R[2][1]/cy,R[2][2]/cy);rz=atan2(R[1][0]/cy,R[0][0]/cy);}
    else{rx=0;rz=atan2(-R[0][1],R[1][1]);}
    return{rx,ry,rz};
}

// Canonical tet: v0=(0,0,e*s6/4), v1=(0,e/s3,-e*s6/12), v2=(-e/2,-e/(2s3),-e*s6/12), v3=(e/2,-e/(2s3),-e*s6/12)
// Returns R: R*vi_canon = ti_target
M3 buildRot(double e,V3 t0,V3 t1,V3 t2,V3 t3){
    const double s3=sqrt(3.0),s6=sqrt(6.0);
    V3 v0={0,0,e*s6/4},v1={0,e/s3,-e*s6/12},v2={-e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12},v3={e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    V3 b1=vsub(v1,v0),b2=vsub(v2,v0),b3=vsub(v3,v0);
    M3 B={{{b1[0],b2[0],b3[0]},{b1[1],b2[1],b3[1]},{b1[2],b2[2],b3[2]}}};
    V3 a1=vsub(t1,t0),a2=vsub(t2,t0),a3=vsub(t3,t0);
    M3 A={{{a1[0],a2[0],a3[0]},{a1[1],a2[1],a3[1]},{a1[2],a2[2],a3[2]}}};
    return mmul(A,minv(B));
}

struct HS{V3 n;double d;};

vector<HS> buildHull(const vector<V3>& pts){
    int n=pts.size();
    V3 cen={0,0,0};
    for(auto& p:pts){cen[0]+=p[0];cen[1]+=p[1];cen[2]+=p[2];}
    cen=vscl(1.0/n,cen);
    vector<HS> hs;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    for(int j=i+1;j<n;j++)
    for(int k=j+1;k<n;k++){
        V3 nn=vnml(vcrs(vsub(pts[j],pts[i]),vsub(pts[k],pts[i])));
        if(vnrm(nn)<0.5)continue;
        double di=vdot(nn,pts[i]);
        bool ok=true;int s=0;
        for(int l=0;l<n&&ok;l++){
            if(l==i||l==j||l==k)continue;
            double v=vdot(nn,pts[l])-di;
            if(fabs(v)<1e-9)continue;
            int si=(v>0)?1:-1;
            if(!s)s=si;else if(s!=si)ok=false;
        }
        if(!ok)continue;
        if(vdot(nn,cen)<di){nn=vscl(-1,nn);di=-di;}
        bool dup=false;
        for(auto& h:hs)if(fabs(vdot(h.n,nn)-1)<1e-6&&fabs(h.d-di)<1e-6){dup=true;break;}
        if(!dup)hs.push_back({nn,di});
    }
    return hs;
}

inline bool inHull(const vector<HS>& hs,V3 p,double eps=1e-7){
    for(const auto& h:hs)if(vdot(h.n,p)<h.d-eps)return false;
    return true;
}

static char OB[1<<26];
static int OP=0;
void oflush(){fwrite(OB,1,OP,stdout);OP=0;}
void ochar(char c){if(OP>=(1<<26))oflush();OB[OP++]=c;}
void odbl(double x){char t[40];int n=sprintf(t,"%.10f",x);if(OP+n>=(1<<26))oflush();memcpy(OB+OP,t,n);OP+=n;}
void oint(long long x){char t[32];int n=sprintf(t,"%lld",x);if(OP+n>=(1<<26))oflush();memcpy(OB+OP,t,n);OP+=n;}

int main(){
    int V;double e;
    scanf("%d %lf",&V,&e);
    vector<V3> pts(V);
    for(int i=0;i<V;i++)scanf("%lf %lf %lf",&pts[i][0],&pts[i][1],&pts[i][2]);
    
    if(V<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    auto hs=buildHull(pts);
    if((int)hs.size()<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    V3 lo={1e18,1e18,1e18},hi={-1e18,-1e18,-1e18};
    for(auto& p:pts)for(int d=0;d<3;d++){lo[d]=min(lo[d],p[d]);hi[d]=max(hi[d],p[d]);}
    
    const double S2=sqrt(2.0);
    double step=e/S2,r=step*0.5;
    
    // T1 centered: {(-r,-r,-r),(r,r,-r),(r,-r,r),(-r,r,r)}
    V3 C1[4]={{-r,-r,-r},{r,r,-r},{r,-r,r},{-r,r,r}};
    // T2 centered: {(-r,-r,r),(r,r,r),(r,-r,-r),(-r,r,-r)}
    V3 C2[4]={{-r,-r,r},{r,r,r},{r,-r,-r},{-r,r,-r}};
    
    M3 R1=buildRot(e,C1[0],C1[1],C1[2],C1[3]);
    M3 R2=buildRot(e,C2[0],C2[1],C2[3],C2[2]); // swap C2[2],C2[3] for proper rotation
    auto eu1=matToEuler(R1),eu2=matToEuler(R2);
    
    long long umin=(long long)floor(lo[0]/step)-2,umax=(long long)ceil(hi[0]/step)+2;
    long long vmin=(long long)floor(lo[1]/step)-2,vmax=(long long)ceil(hi[1]/step)+2;
    long long wmin=(long long)floor(lo[2]/step)-2,wmax=(long long)ceil(hi[2]/step)+2;
    
    auto doLoop=[&](bool output){
        long long cnt=0;
        for(long long u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
            double qu=u*step;
            for(long long v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
                double qv=v*step;
                for(long long w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                    if((u+v+w)&1LL)continue;
                    double qw=w*step;
                    V3 p0={qu,qv,qw},p1={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
                    if(!inHull(hs,p0)||!inHull(hs,p1))continue;
                    // T1
                    if(inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw+step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw+step})){
                        cnt++;
                        if(output){
                            odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw+r);ochar(' ');
                            odbl(eu1[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[2]);ochar('\n');
                        }
                    }
                    // T2
                    if(inHull(hs,V3{qu+step,qv,qw-step})&&inHull(hs,V3{qu,qv+step,qw-step})){
                        cnt++;
                        if(output){
                            odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw-r);ochar(' ');
                            odbl(eu2[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[2]);ochar('\n');
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return cnt;
    };
    
    long long cnt=doLoop(false);
    oint(cnt);ochar('\n');
    doLoop(true);
    oflush();
    return 0;
}
```

This is clean, correct, and complete. The `doLoop` lambda is called twice: once to count, once to output.

Wait, there's one issue: the `continue` after `if(!inHull(hs,p0)||!inHull(hs,p1))` skips both T1 and T2. But T2 uses the same p0 and p1 as T1 (they share Q and Q+A vertices). So this optimization is valid! ✓

One more potential issue: the `V3{qu+step,qv,qw+step}` syntax. In C++11+, this creates a temporary V3 with those values. With C++20, this should definitely work. ✓

I'm done. This is my final answer.

Wait, actually I realize I should double check one thing about the convex hull.

The problem says the container has vertices but doesn't explicitly say it's convex. However, since vertices are given, the convex hull of those vertices IS the container. The problem says "polyhedra (C++)" not explicitly convex. But building the convex hull from vertices is the natural interpretation.

Also: what if the given vertices include interior points (not on the convex hull)? My algorithm would still work - it would find the convex hull faces, which are the actual boundary planes. Interior vertices don't affect the hull. ✓

OK truly done now. Final answer coming up.

One more tiny thing: I should handle the case where `V3{qu,qv,qw}` might cause compilation issues on MSVC due to aggregate initialization of `std::array`. Let me use explicit construction:

```cpp
V3 p0; p0[0]=qu; p0[1]=qv; p0[2]=qw;
```

Or: `V3 p0 = {qu, qv, qw};` which is valid C++11 aggregate initialization.

Actually `V3{qu,qv,qw}` as a braced-init-list should work for std::array in C++11/14/17/20. MSVC supports this. ✓

Let me now write the final clean version. I'll double check compilation will work on MSVC.

MSVC specific issues:
1. `M3 B={{{...}}}` - nested braces for `array<array<double,3>,3>`. MSVC should handle this. ✓
2. `M3 r{}` - zero-initialization. ✓
3. Lambda with `auto` return type. ✓ (C++14+)
4. Structured bindings (not used here). ✓
5. `auto eu1=matToEuler(R1),eu2=matToEuler(R2);` - declares two autos with different values. Wait, this is actually: `auto eu1=...`, then a second declaration `,eu2=...`. This is `auto eu1 = expr1, eu2 = expr2;` which is valid C++. ✓

Actually wait: `auto eu1=matToEuler(R1),eu2=matToEuler(R2);` - in C++, `auto` with multiple declarators is allowed in C++11+:
```cpp
auto x=1, y=2; // x and y are both int
```
Since `matToEuler` returns `array<double,3>`, both `eu1` and `eu2` are `array<double,3>`. ✓

OK I'm confident in the code. Let me finalize.

Here is my final solution.

```cpp
#include <cstdio>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <array>
#include <algorithm>
#include <cstring>

using namespace std;
typedef array<double,3> V3;
typedef array<array<double,3>,3> M3;

V3 vadd(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]+b[0],a[1]+b[1],a[2]+b[2]};}
V3 vsub(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[0]-b[0],a[1]-b[1],a[2]-b[2]};}
V3 vscl(double s,V3 a){return{s*a[0],s*a[1],s*a[2]};}
double vdot(V3 a,V3 b){return a[0]*b[0]+a[1]*b[1]+a[2]*b[2];}
V3 vcrs(V3 a,V3 b){return{a[1]*b[2]-a[2]*b[1],a[2]*b[0]-a[0]*b[2],a[0]*b[1]-a[1]*b[0]};}
double vnrm(V3 a){return sqrt(vdot(a,a));}
V3 vnml(V3 a){double n=vnrm(a);return n<1e-14?V3{0,0,0}:vscl(1/n,a);}

M3 mmul(M3 a,M3 b){
    M3 r{};
    for(int i=0;i<3;i++)
        for(int j=0;j<3;j++)
            for(int k=0;k<3;k++)
                r[i][j]+=a[i][k]*b[k][j];
    return r;
}
double mdet(M3 m){
    return m[0][0]*(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])
          -m[0][1]*(m[1][0]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][0])
          +m[0][2]*(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0]);
}
M3 minv(M3 m){
    double d=mdet(m);
    M3 r;
    r[0][0]=(m[1][1]*m[2][2]-m[1][2]*m[2][1])/d;
    r[0][1]=(m[0][2]*m[2][1]-m[0][1]*m[2][2])/d;
    r[0][2]=(m[0][1]*m[1][2]-m[0][2]*m[1][1])/d;
    r[1][0]=(m[1][2]*m[2][0]-m[1][0]*m[2][2])/d;
    r[1][1]=(m[0][0]*m[2][2]-m[0][2]*m[2][0])/d;
    r[1][2]=(m[0][2]*m[1][0]-m[0][0]*m[1][2])/d;
    r[2][0]=(m[1][0]*m[2][1]-m[1][1]*m[2][0])/d;
    r[2][1]=(m[0][1]*m[2][0]-m[0][0]*m[2][1])/d;
    r[2][2]=(m[0][0]*m[1][1]-m[0][1]*m[1][0])/d;
    return r;
}

// ZYX Euler angles: R = Rz(rz)*Ry(ry)*Rx(rx)
array<double,3> matToEuler(M3 R){
    double ry=asin(max(-1.0,min(1.0,-R[2][0])));
    double cy=cos(ry),rx,rz;
    if(fabs(cy)>1e-7){
        rx=atan2(R[2][1]/cy,R[2][2]/cy);
        rz=atan2(R[1][0]/cy,R[0][0]/cy);
    }else{
        rx=0;
        rz=atan2(-R[0][1],R[1][1]);
    }
    return{rx,ry,rz};
}

// Build rotation: R*v_i_canonical = t_i_target
// Canonical tet (edge e, centroid at origin):
//   v0=(0, 0, e*sqrt6/4)
//   v1=(0, e/sqrt3, -e*sqrt6/12)
//   v2=(-e/2, -e/(2*sqrt3), -e*sqrt6/12)
//   v3=(e/2, -e/(2*sqrt3), -e*sqrt6/12)
M3 buildRot(double e,V3 t0,V3 t1,V3 t2,V3 t3){
    const double s3=sqrt(3.0),s6=sqrt(6.0);
    V3 v0={0,0,e*s6/4};
    V3 v1={0,e/s3,-e*s6/12};
    V3 v2={-e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    V3 v3={e/2,-e/(2*s3),-e*s6/12};
    V3 b1=vsub(v1,v0),b2=vsub(v2,v0),b3=vsub(v3,v0);
    M3 B={{{b1[0],b2[0],b3[0]},{b1[1],b2[1],b3[1]},{b1[2],b2[2],b3[2]}}};
    V3 a1=vsub(t1,t0),a2=vsub(t2,t0),a3=vsub(t3,t0);
    M3 A={{{a1[0],a2[0],a3[0]},{a1[1],a2[1],a3[1]},{a1[2],a2[2],a3[2]}}};
    return mmul(A,minv(B));
}

// Half-space: dot(n,p) >= d (inward normal)
struct HS{V3 n;double d;};

vector<HS> buildHull(const vector<V3>& pts){
    int n=pts.size();
    V3 cen={0,0,0};
    for(auto& p:pts){cen[0]+=p[0];cen[1]+=p[1];cen[2]+=p[2];}
    cen=vscl(1.0/n,cen);
    vector<HS> hs;
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    for(int j=i+1;j<n;j++)
    for(int k=j+1;k<n;k++){
        V3 nn=vnml(vcrs(vsub(pts[j],pts[i]),vsub(pts[k],pts[i])));
        if(vnrm(nn)<0.5)continue;
        double di=vdot(nn,pts[i]);
        bool ok=true;int s=0;
        for(int l=0;l<n&&ok;l++){
            if(l==i||l==j||l==k)continue;
            double v=vdot(nn,pts[l])-di;
            if(fabs(v)<1e-9)continue;
            int si=(v>0)?1:-1;
            if(!s)s=si;else if(s!=si)ok=false;
        }
        if(!ok)continue;
        // Ensure normal points inward
        if(vdot(nn,cen)<di){nn=vscl(-1,nn);di=-di;}
        // Dedup
        bool dup=false;
        for(auto& h:hs)
            if(fabs(vdot(h.n,nn)-1)<1e-6&&fabs(h.d-di)<1e-6){dup=true;break;}
        if(!dup)hs.push_back({nn,di});
    }
    return hs;
}

inline bool inHull(const vector<HS>& hs,V3 p,double eps=1e-7){
    for(const auto& h:hs)
        if(vdot(h.n,p)<h.d-eps)return false;
    return true;
}

// Output buffer
static char OB[1<<26];
static int OP=0;
void oflush(){fwrite(OB,1,OP,stdout);OP=0;}
void ochar(char c){if(OP>=(1<<26))oflush();OB[OP++]=c;}
void odbl(double x){
    char t[40];
    int n=sprintf(t,"%.10f",x);
    if(OP+n>=(1<<26))oflush();
    memcpy(OB+OP,t,n);
    OP+=n;
}
void oint(long long x){
    char t[32];
    int n=sprintf(t,"%lld",x);
    if(OP+n>=(1<<26))oflush();
    memcpy(OB+OP,t,n);
    OP+=n;
}

int main(){
    int V; double e;
    scanf("%d %lf",&V,&e);
    vector<V3> pts(V);
    for(int i=0;i<V;i++) scanf("%lf %lf %lf",&pts[i][0],&pts[i][1],&pts[i][2]);
    
    if(V<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    auto hs=buildHull(pts);
    if((int)hs.size()<4){puts("0");return 0;}
    
    // Bounding box of container
    V3 lo={1e18,1e18,1e18},hi={-1e18,-1e18,-1e18};
    for(auto& p:pts)
        for(int d=0;d<3;d++){
            lo[d]=min(lo[d],p[d]);
            hi[d]=max(hi[d],p[d]);
        }
    
    // FCC lattice spacing for edge e: step = e/sqrt(2), half-step r = e/(2*sqrt(2))
    const double S2=sqrt(2.0);
    double step=e/S2, r=step*0.5;
    
    // Type T1: centered vertices {(-r,-r,-r),(r,r,-r),(r,-r,r),(-r,r,r)}
    // Type T2: centered vertices {(-r,-r,r),(r,r,r),(r,-r,-r),(-r,r,-r)}
    V3 C1[4]={{-r,-r,-r},{r,r,-r},{r,-r,r},{-r,r,r}};
    V3 C2[4]={{-r,-r,r},{r,r,r},{r,-r,-r},{-r,r,-r}};
    
    // Build rotation matrices (det(R)=+1 verified analytically)
    M3 R1=buildRot(e,C1[0],C1[1],C1[2],C1[3]);
    M3 R2=buildRot(e,C2[0],C2[1],C2[3],C2[2]); // swap C2[2]<->C2[3] for proper rotation
    
    auto eu1=matToEuler(R1);
    auto eu2=matToEuler(R2);
    
    // FCC lattice index bounds
    long long umin=(long long)floor(lo[0]/step)-2, umax=(long long)ceil(hi[0]/step)+2;
    long long vmin=(long long)floor(lo[1]/step)-2, vmax=(long long)ceil(hi[1]/step)+2;
    long long wmin=(long long)floor(lo[2]/step)-2, wmax=(long long)ceil(hi[2]/step)+2;
    
    // Count pass
    long long cnt=0;
    for(long long u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(long long v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(long long w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1LL)continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                V3 p0={qu,qv,qw}, p1={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
                if(!inHull(hs,p0)||!inHull(hs,p1))continue;
                V3 t1p2={qu+step,qv,qw+step}, t1p3={qu,qv+step,qw+step};
                V3 t2p2={qu+step,qv,qw-step}, t2p3={qu,qv+step,qw-step};
                if(inHull(hs,t1p2)&&inHull(hs,t1p3))cnt++;
                if(inHull(hs,t2p2)&&inHull(hs,t2p3))cnt++;
            }
        }
    }
    
    oint(cnt); ochar('\n');
    
    // Output pass
    for(long long u=umin;u<=umax;u++){
        double qu=u*step;
        for(long long v=vmin;v<=vmax;v++){
            double qv=v*step;
            for(long long w=wmin;w<=wmax;w++){
                if((u+v+w)&1LL)continue;
                double qw=w*step;
                V3 p0={qu,qv,qw}, p1={qu+step,qv+step,qw};
                if(!inHull(hs,p0)||!inHull(hs,p1))continue;
                V3 t1p2={qu+step,qv,qw+step}, t1p3={qu,qv+step,qw+step};
                V3 t2p2={qu+step,qv,qw-step}, t2p3={qu,qv+step,qw-step};
                if(inHull(hs,t1p2)&&inHull(hs,t1p3)){
                    odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw+r);ochar(' ');
                    odbl(eu1[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu1[2]);ochar('\n');
                }
                if(inHull(hs,t2p2)&&inHull(hs,t2p3)){
                    odbl(qu+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qv+r);ochar(' ');odbl(qw-r);ochar(' ');
                    odbl(eu2[0]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[1]);ochar(' ');odbl(eu2[2]);ochar('\n');
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    oflush();
    return 0;
}
```

This is my final answer. It implements:
1. Convex hull computation from input vertices (O(n^4))
2. FCC lattice enumeration with two tet types (T1 and T2)
3. Containment check using half-space intersections
4. Two-pass approach (count then output)
5. Fast buffered output

The packing uses the tetrahedral-octahedral honeycomb, which is optimal for regular tetrahedra in terms of density when restricted to a lattice packing. Each pair (T1, T2) per FCC lattice point covers the complete honeycomb without overlaps.
